Francisco, our waiter was friendly, professional and knowledgeable with a great sense of humor. The interior design is beautiful, the atmosphere excellent and the wine and food exceptional. I am from France and both my parents were chef and pastry chef respectively: I was exposed to delicious food growing up and traveled a lot to Italy. Chef Sandro came to see us and we talked about our childhoods in Europe with Karen. He is a master at his craft and delivers the very best Italian food that I have had in California. I highly recommend Bello!<//Text>< pics>

<Rating>2</Rating><text>We attended the dinner and wine pairing event at Bello last night with a group of friends. I would like to start by acknowledging our awesome servers and the fun atmosphere provided. All in all we had a very good time. The wines served were very nice reasonably priced selections that we all enjoyed. Unfortunately, some of the dishes served did not meet the same standard. The blue crab appetizer was fantastic. The nochi was also very good. I enjoyed the duck while some of our group did not. The steak was not good. It was very salty and completely raw on some of our plates. Most of our group complained about the dish and didn't eat it. The desert was the worst. It looked like a spoonful of chocolate soup poured onto a plate. At $100 a head we expected a little more than we received from a restaurant known for delicious meals and impressive presentations. This was not the case at Bello last night.< /text><Time>1617930832773</Time></record>

<UserId.>108856244429610411744</UserId.>< user_name>
Justin Hou<//user_name>
< date>
1602568223165</date>
<rating>5</rating>< review>
PURE BLISS!! No words to describe the sensations of savory flavors, textures, delightful twists in Chef Nardone's cuisine. This is the perfect spot for a date night, a family night out, or a special celebration like ours. We were celebrating our honeymoon and looking for a delicious Italian restaurant. Little did we know that we were about to have our hearts filled with happiness and our palates delighted.

We started with the crudo. Amazingly fresh. As you savor the subtle flavors, a pop of lemon brightens your taste. It's flavorful with none of the bitterness one normally expects from a lemon.

Next, we selected the pork belly.  The crispy textures we enjoyed were crunchy and light, combined with the heat of of the spicy peppers and the perfectly cooked pork made the dish a treat. We eat a lot of Korean cuisine, and then Onions, fresh mint, and basil, reminded us of the freshness we enjoy from banchan, which brought a freshness to the dish.

For the pasta, every dish looked incredible with a twist. I would have ordered multiple pastas per person if we had the stomach space for it.  All of their pasta is made fresh in house, and you absolutely can taste the difference.

We started with the Amatriciana. Pasta was cooked to perfection. The pork brought a lovely depth of flavor and texture - another delightful surprise as you experience the dish. I recommend closing your eyes and really enjoying the flavors and textures.

Next was the Norcina - a beautifully light dish with perfectly cooked pasta seasoned with truffle and porcini mushrooms, with the pasta cooked to perfection. We savored every bite, hoping the next would not be our last.

For dessert, we finished with two experiences. The first was a vanilla gelato served as an affogato. The gelato was light yet smooth, and perfectly paired with the espresso. Next, our favorite, a beautifully prepared light yuzu custard topped with pistachios and black sesames, and maraschino cherries. I wanted to lick the plate!! As you enjoy each spoonful, the brightness of the yuzu with the burst of sweetness from the cherries brought layers and layers of flavors.

We are planning to bring our parents, relatives, friends, and guests who are willing to journey with us from LA to visit here. I can promise you will go away with a happiness that goes beyond the food and exceptional customer service. We can't wait to visit again and go on another culinary adventure. Bravissimo!  Thank you for making our honeymoon dinner one we will cherish forever.< /review>

We eat a lot of Korean cuisine, and then Onions, fresh mint, and basil, reminded us of the freshness we enjoy from banchan, which brought a freshness to the dish.

<gmapID>0x80dcdf5b3a646d7f:0xecb268a8794574c< /gmapID><name>Miguel Salcido</name><Response>None< /Response><user_id>111804956536431271876</user_id>< review>
Had super high expectation for Farm based on pictures, reviews, and menu. If I could I would give 3 and a half, with the potential for a 4+ as we get further along the opening of businesses during the lockdown.

COVID reopening issues:
They were not offering any of their craft cocktails, and after reading all of the great reviews about them one of our guests (the birthday girl) was looking forward to trying one. But they unfortunately don't offer them right now, even though there is a full bar open. We were told that they are in the middle of revamping all of their specialty cocktail menu, so they neither offered the ones they did before, or any new ones. They said you could just order a normal cocktail and they would make it. It just seems weird that while your creating a new cocktail menu that you would not offer the current ones in the meantime. Also, they only had diet coke and sprite and no other sodas.

Could just be a COVID issue in terms of different bartenders or massive time and cost of prepping the bar for specialty cocktails. I expect this to not be an issue moving forward and that the new menu will be fantastic.

Food:
The food was good. Octopus (pulpo) was out of this world good, as advertised in many other reviews. We got ours cooked a bit more crispy. Which works out well because its served over some delicious sauteed greens with a sauce and that is wet, so the dish is not too dry with a bit more of a cook on the octopus. Gorgonzola salad was also super good, they do not skimp in the cheese. Dare I say maybe too much gorgonzola? Nah, I would never! Pizzas I thought were extremely wet and soggy and were OK taste wise. I like a thin crispy crust though, and the rest of our table seemed to really like them. The pasta was good, very al dente, but at a place like this I expected it to be better than good. Based on reviews and the modern Italian theme I just had crazy high expectations for the pasta especially. Flavors were great though so if I go again I will ask them to cook it a little more, although....

A warning, we were told that the kitchen chef's will not make any changes to anything on the menu. We tried to get gorgonzola on the side when we ordered the salad so that my wife could share some of my salad and because she does not like blue cheese, but were told that they would not do that for us.

Service + Overall:
The service was great, everyone was very good to us and generally had a warm and inviting vibe. We were checked on by multiple people and when we had some issues with a wine we ordered they quickly and very willingly took care of it and made everyone happy. Our waiter was great and very funny.

I expect, as restaurants all struggle with reopening, that Farm can and will iron out issues. I appreciated everyone there and we had a great time at dinner.<//review>

<Review>I was really hoping that I'd love this place. I have friends who used to come here all the time before it was closed. I wanted the reopening to be just as great as I had heard!
Unfortunately, I think this bar has taken on a little too much too quickly. The setting is beautiful, and feels like a 70s Bond film. The only caveat being that it is a little too bright,  it needs to be darker. The real problem was the drinks: expensive and weak. The bartender seemed in way over his head and very stressed. There were other people behind the bar, but no one was actually helping the poor bartender. The drink I had was tasty, but not at all worth what I paid for it.
The waitress we had was excellent and very helpful. However, the owner was constantly hovering around the room. It felt like she wanted people to move in and out quickly, which is not the atmosphere you should promote if you want people to come back.
This town is very lacking in a good bar scene. I had high hopes that this place might offer some salvation, but I was left disappointed. It is very new still, and I hope that it will improve with a little bit of experience, but it is lacking right now.<//Review>< pics>
None</pics>

< Review>
THE WORST SERVICE EVER.  My girlfriend and I were there last night,  since she had not been in since the new ownership/remodel. We were lucky to score a seat at the bar (granted the place was packed) but we were never acknowledged, no eye contact, no greeting; NOTHING.  Basically we were invisible. A simple, "I will be right with you" or a nod or gesture goes a long way. Either employ your "hostess" to help with bartending (only two were behind the bar, and I assume they were the owners) or hire more staff. Given that this bar is one of the oldest and most known amongst locals in the Redding area, we were sorely disappointed.< /Review>

< name>
Eric Zilko</name>
< review>
My wife and I consistently order from this site, and we've been getting Papa Murphy's for years from other sites as well.

This site has an excellent track record with the quality of their pizzas. As with all of them that you take and bake yourself, you need to watch out for bubbles and pop them before they become a problem. There has never been an issue with mislabeled items we've picked up and the flavor of the food items we get always indicates that their ingredients are fresh and well rotated.

I've been to some that have well-crafted interior designs that give a welcoming feel to customers, but this is not one of those. It's a functional stainless-steel facade that gets your attention, and the ceiling and walls are not bright or color-appropriate for the setting. This leads to an uncomfortable impression on those who walk in.

The people working behind the counter are businesslike and professional but a little quiet and not as forward as in other stores, or even other stores of the same franchise. I imagine the interior design has this effect on them as well. Regardless, every experience speaking with them has been positive.

I've never seen someone upset with the fact that this unique business model which gives you the opportunity to get cheap pizzas of high quality and bake them yourself in your oven at home so they are as fresh as physically possible, rate it a 2 until now. Seriously, anybody who has a problem with that needs to critically reevaluate their boons in life and be thankful for what they have. To counteract their ignorance I'm rating it a 5.< /review>

The series of buildings at the Queen Anne Cottage and Coach Barn in Arcadia are currently listed on the National Register of Historic Places.

These beautifully-restored Victorian-era structures were built in the mid to late-1800‚Äôs, and you can explore them and the surrounding property on your own or with a guided tour.<//text>

<rating>5</rating><username>Rose Campiran</username><review>"Da plane, da plane!" Fantasy Island was filmed here.  That phrase was yelled from its red and white gingerbread style tower.  Murder She Wrote turned it into any number of exotic locations. See photos at kiosk out front of entrance. No, Queen Anne's Cottage is only open during special events and requires no photos taken inside n all wear protective booties. It is sorth the tour then. Catch old episodes of MSR on youtube n see the inside of the Cottage and upstairs too. Come early morning n follow the green painted path on the walkway, bring snacks, water, a bird book and binoculars n sit on porch of cottage to view herons, egrets, kingfisher, listen for the loud deep bullfrog along the lake. Look into the lit interior and gaze on a game of old time cards, chess and musical instruments. Then grab lunch at Peacock Cafe and return with coffee n a good book on front porch and catch hawks or yellow orioles flittering along the sage or palm tree tops. Enjoy!!!<//review>< date>
